Overall, a really unique hotel, but for the price, really should step up hygiene.

posted:Posted October 2, 2023
msg:It's our 1st time staying in Seclusive, and we chose to celebrate my 50th birthday here (we're from Singapore). In our 6 days trip in Shanghai, this is the 3rd hotel we've stayed for 3 nights. We booked 2 rooms - a suite and a king-sized bedroom.  Talk about the downside first.  The suite (on the 2nd floor) is spacious with a terrace, however the king-sized bedroom (on the ground floor) was extremely small, it will not be suitable if you're a 6 footer at all (you'd probably be knocking your knee to alot of things).  Since it is an old structured building, the sewerage system is no good (toilets in both our rooms were choked and needed attention).  The staircase to the level 2 was really steep with uneven carpet. They should also plan to hire more (& younger) housekeeping staff as cleaning up the rooms takes longer than expected, we waited on the day of check-in as well as when we were out for lunch (2 hours).  Now on the good things!  Location is great as it is walking distance to alot of shops, cafes, restaurants.  We reckon that this is a 'hot' and 'social influencer' locality with lotsa crowd taking photos and vids.  What made the stay MOST PLEASANT and MEMORABLE is the staff named Ace, true to his name - he was truly a superstar with top-notch service and attitude, the type you'd think never exist in this world!  From settling the laundry (with an external vendor), booking cars, restaurants reservations, birthday-surprise decor to the room,  all coordination with external vendors and many more!  Last but not least - with a bright smile at all times!  If at all we decide to be back, its only because of Ace!

msg:"The never-fading Shanghai Dream" - Magic Capital is known as the road to celebrities that "condenses the century-old history of modern Shanghai", and is also the first national historical and cultural street "Wukang Road"; The old building has ushered in the transformation of the new century, and transformed into [Shanghai Seclusion and Prosperous Wukang Road Mansion] (20 guest rooms with different characteristics) open to the outside world; here it condenses the perfect fusion of French delicacy and Shanghai-style charm and reinterprets it.

The French phoenix tree on Wukang Road is quiet and beautiful; after passing through the street with the shadow of phoenix trees, you arrive at the entrance of the hotel. The low-key golden signboard is placed on the light-colored courtyard wall, and the thick dark metal door is pushed open, and the courtyard opens in front of you. The whole old building has a "symmetrical" plane, one black and one white: the left side is a bright white space "French restaurant BLANCHE"; the right side is a quiet Shanghai-style a**osphere, a dark and restrained world, with mystery and darkness in front of us Expand (the foreground is set here).

This time I stayed in the "Elegant Terrace Room". The combination of "copper" elements and velvet and other materials in the room is decorated with French classical charm. Every corner is like an oil painting. bustling". Here we would like to thank "Xiao Xu" who served us throughout the whole process. It is really physical work to move large luggage up and down!
